    The above text provides various traditional remedies for toothache and related conditions.

    1. For toothache due to wind and cold:
      Grind the following into a powder: Bai Zhi, Xi Xin, Liang Jiang, Bi Ba, Chuan Jiao, Xiang Fu Zi, and Bee Honeycomb, each in equal parts. Use three qian (a measure) with water to decoct and gargle, or apply it.

    2. Pepper and Salt Powder:
      For pain from cavities: Grind together one qian each of Chuan Jiao, white salt, and Bee Honeycomb. Mix with three stalks of green onion, decoct in water, and use hot for gargling and cold for spitting out.

    3. Beecomb Powder (from "Hui Chun"):
      For pain from wind and cavities, which is unbearable. Grind the ingredients and decoct in a mixture of water and vinegar for hot gargling and cold spitting out.

    4. Ten Whole and Greatly Supplementing Decoction:
      For painful hollow teeth: Use one qian each of Ren Shen, Bai Zhu (stir-fried), Bai Shao (stir-fried), peeled Bai Fu Ling, processed Huang Qi, Dang Gui, processed Gan Cao, Shu Di, and Chuan Xiong, with two fen of Gui Xin. Add two slices of ginger and three jujubes, then decoct for consumption.

    5. Ma Huang, Fu Zi, and Xi Xin Decoction (from Zhongjing):
      For yang deficiency toothaches: Use two liang each of Ma Huang (cut into sections) and Xi Xin (cleaned), and one piece of Fu Zi. Decoct with water for consumption.

    6. Ge Hua Jie Cheng Decoction:
      For toothache caused by excessive drinking: Combine five fen each of Ge Hua, Sha Ren, Bai Dou Kou, Chen Pi, Ren Shen, and Bai Fu Ling, and two fen each of Shen Qu (stir-fried), Bai Zhu (stir-fried), Gan Jiang, and Qing Pi (peeled and stir-fried), along with Ze Xie. Decoct for consumption.[45p]

    　　天南星丸　治痰火上逆牙疼。
    　　天南星炮　硫黄研　石膏研　硝石研，各等分　　右为末，面糊为丸，如梧桐子大，每服二十丸，空心、日午、临卧三时服。
    　　犀角地黄汤　治阴虚火盛牙疼。
    　　生犀角镑　牡丹皮各二钱五分　白芍药二钱　生地黄一两五钱　水煎服。
    　　凉膈散　治胃火牙肿痛，牙宣。
    　　黄芩酒炒　栀子炒　薄荷各一两　连翘四两　大黄酒浸　芒硝　甘草各二两　　右共为末，每服五钱。

    　　消风散　治风火牙疼。
    　　荆芥穗　制甘草　陈皮　厚朴姜汁炒　藿香　蝉蜕　人参　白僵蚕炒　茯苓　防风　芎藭　羌活　　右，水煎服。

    　　巴豆丸　一名一笑散。治虫牙疼痛，蚀孔空虚。　　巴豆一枚　花椒五十粒，细研
    　　右为极细末，饭丸黍米大，绵包塞蛀孔。
    　　藜芦散　治虫牙疼痛。
    　　藜芦不拘多少　为末塞孔中，勿令咽汁，有涎吐之，大有神效。[46p]

    Heavenly South Star Pill treats phlegm and fire rising causing toothache.

    Powder heavenly south star, sulfur, gypsum, nitrate, all in equal parts. Grind to a fine powder, mix with flour to form pills the size of a Chinese parasol seed. Take twenty pills each time on an empty stomach, at noon, and before bed.

    Rhino Horn and Rehmannia Decoction treats yin deficiency and excessive fire causing toothache.

    Use two and a half qian of powdered rhino horn, peony root; two qian of white peony; and one and a half liang of raw rehmannia. Boil in water and take.

    Cool the Stomach Powder treats stomach fire causing swollen and painful gums, and tooth sensitivity.

    Use one liang each of yellow qin wine fried, gardenia fried, and mint; four liang of forsythia; and two liang each of rhubarb, sodium sulfate, and licorice, soaked in yellow wine. Grind into a powder, take five qian each time.

    Dispersing Wind Powder treats wind and fire toothache.

    Use the spikes of schizopepon, prepared licorice, dried tangerine peel, thick pericarp fried in ginger juice, patchouli, cicada molting, ginseng, fried silkworms, poria, saposhnikovia, and qianghuo. Boil in water and take.

    Castor Bean Pill, also known as One Smile Powder, treats tooth pain from cavities.

    Take one castor bean and fifty grains of Sichuan pepper, ground finely. Make into a very fine powder, form into pills the size of millet, and stuff into cavities.

    Alismatis Powder treats insect-induced tooth pain.

    Use an unspecified amount of alisma, grind to powder and stuff into the cavity, avoiding swallowing any juice; expectorate saliva. It has remarkable efficacy.[46p]

    　　韭子汤　治虫牙。
    　　韭菜子一撮

    　　真琥珀研　犀角屑生用，各一钱　人参去芦　酸枣仁去皮，研　茯神去皮木　辰砂研，各二钱　片脑研，一字　　右为细末，研匀，炼蜜和为膏，以磁器收贮。候其疾作，每服一弹子大，以麦门冬去心浓煎汤化下，一日连进五服。[47p]

    Leek Seed Soup: Treats worm-eaten teeth.
    Take a pinch of leek seeds. Place in a bowl, burn to create smoke, and using a small bamboo tube split at the bottom into four openings, cover the opening with paper shaped like a trumpet to guide the smoke to the decayed tooth. If it’s a lower tooth, rinse with a concentrated decoction of the seeds; the worms will come out by themselves.

    North Jujube Decoction: Treats rampant tooth decay.
    Take one pitted North jujube, insert a weight of arsenic into the jujube and heat to keep it intact, grind finely, and apply a small amount to the affected area.

    Three Immortals Powder: Treats rampant tooth decay which can cause immediate death if it rots.
    Three parts of verdigris, one part of musk, and one piece of white sediment from a woman’s urine bucket, calcined, about four grams in total. Grind to a very fine powder and apply, but do not use too much.

    Rhinoceros Horn and Cimicifuga Decoction: Treats wind-heat toothache.
    Seven grams of powdered rhinoceros horn, five and a half grams each of ledebouriella and notopterygium, two and a half grams each of angelica, scutellaria, and white peony, and one and a half grams of licorice, along with five grams of cimicifuga. Decoct seven grams in water for each dosage.

    Amber and Rhinoceros Horn Ointment: Treats fiery tooth pain and elevated dental sensitivity.
    Finely grind real amber and fresh rhinoceros horn shavings, each one gram. Remove the husk from ginseng, pit from sour jujube seeds, and peel from poria, and grind together, each two grams. Grind the plates of brain powder finely. Mix these into a fine powder evenly, then refine with honey to form an ointment and store in a ceramic container. When symptoms arise, take a piece the size of a bullet, dissolve in a concentrated decoction of lily bulbs, and take five doses in one day.[47p]

    　　加减甘露饮 【《本事方》】 　治胃热牙宣。　　熟地黄　生地黄　天门冬去心　黄芩　枳壳　枇杷叶去毛　茵陈　金钗石斛各一两　甘草　犀角镑，各五钱　　右为末，每服二钱，水一盏，煎至七分，去滓，食后临卧温服。小儿一服分作两服，更斟酌与之。

    Jia Jian Gan Lu Yin (Sweet Dew Decoction)
    This is used to treat stomach heat and toothaches.
    Ingredients:

    • 1 ounce of cooked Rehmannia
    • 1 ounce of raw Rehmannia
    • 1 ounce of Asparagus (remove the heart)
    • 1 ounce of Scutellaria
    • 1 ounce of Bitter Orange Peel
    • 1 ounce of Loquat Leaf (remove hairs)
    • 1 ounce of Artemisia
    • 1 ounce of Dendrobium
    • 0.5 ounces of Licorice
    • 0.5 ounces of Rhinoceros Horn
      Grind these into a powder. For each dose, take 0.6 ounces, mix with a cup of water, and boil until reduced by a third. Strain and take warm after meals or before lying down. For children, divide the dose into two and adjust accordingly.

    She Fan San (Musk and Alum Powder)
    Used to treat rampant toothache and severe symptoms.

    • A small amount of Musk
    • 0.5 ounces of Alum
    • 0.25 ounces of Verdigris
    • 0.1 ounces of raw Alumen
      Grind the above into a fine powder and apply to the affected tooth area.

    An Shen Wan (Calm the Kidney Pill)

    Huanglian Xiaodu San - Treats real heat tooth pain.
    Huanglian (prepared) and Qianghuo each 1 fen; Huangqin, Huangbo, Zhigeng, Gaoben, Fangji each 5 fen; Dangguiwei, Lianqiao, Fangfeng, Duhuo, and Zhi Mu (prepared) and Shengdi each 4 fen; Huangqi, Sumu, Chenpi, Zexie each 2 fen; Renshen and Gancao each 3 fen. Prepare by decocting in water.

    Da Chengqi Tang - Treats stomach heat tooth pain.
    Dahuang 4 liang (taels), soaked in wine; Mangxiao 3 he (catty); Houpu ½ sheng (liters), stir-fried in ginger decoction; Zhi Shi 5 pieces, stir-fried; prepare by decocting in water.

    Tiao Wei Chengqi Tang - Treats the above condition.
    Dahuang soaked in wine, Mangxiao each 1 liang; Gancao, roasted, 5 qian (money); take a small amount warm.
    Yue Ju Wan - Treats liver fire and anger tooth pain.
    Xiangfu (Fructus Cyperi) stir-fried with vinegar; Cangzhu (Atractylodes) soaked in rice water; Fuxiong, Zhi Zhi (Gardenia) stir-fried black, Shenyu stir-fried, each equal portions; prepare into a powder, form into pills the size of a small bean, take 100 pills each time.
    Buzhong Yiqi Tang - Treats qi deficiency tooth pain.
    Renshen and Gancao (roasted) each 1 qian; Shengma 5 fen; Danggui (body) and Baizhu (stir-fried) Chenpi and Chaihu each 5 fen; Huangqi (honey roasted) 1.5 qian; 3 slices of ginger, 2 dates; prepare by decocting in water and take warm.[49p]

    　　茵陈散　治牙齿疼痛，外面赤肿疼痛，及去骨槽风热。　　茵陈　连翘　半夏　荆芥穗　麻黄　升麻　黄芩　牡丹皮　射干　羌活　独活　大黄炮　薄荷　僵蚕各二钱半　细辛五钱　牵牛一两　　右为细末，每服三钱。水一盏，先煎汤熟，下药末搅一搅，急泻出，食后连滓热服。[50p]

    Gui Pi Decoction: Used for blood not returning to the channels, presenting with dental bleeding.

    Ingredients: 1 qian of Yuanzhi, 2 qians each of Ren Shen, Fu Ling, Huang Qi, Bai Zhu, Zao Ren, Long Yan Rou, 5 fen each of Mu Xiang, Zhi Gan Cao, and Dang Gui. Boil with ginger and jujube water.

    Liu Wei Wan: Used for deficiency of water and excess fire causing toothache.

    Ingredients: 8 liang of Shou Di, steamed with wine; 4 liang each of Shan Yu Rou and Fu Ling mixed with milk; 3 liang each of Shan Yao, Ze Xie, and Mu Dan Pi; 1 liang each of Fu Zi and Rou Gui. Make into pills the size of a tung seed, and take with salty warm water.

    Ba Wei Wan: Used for deficiency fire in the Ming Men (Gate of Life) leading to toothache.

    Ingredients: 8 liang of Shou Di mixed with sand and steamed nine times; 4 liang each of Shan Yu Rou and Shan Yao moistened with wine; 3 liang each of Fu Ling mixed with milk, Dan Pi, and Ze Xie; 1 liang each of Fu Zi and Rou Gui.

    Yin Chen San: Used for toothache, with external redness, swelling, and wind-heat in the bone sockets.

    Ingredients: 2.5 qians each of Yin Chen, Lian Qiao, Ban Xia, Jing Jie Sui, Ma Huang, Sheng Ma, Huang Qin, Mu Dan Pi, She Gan, Qiang Huo, Du Huo, Da Huang Pao, Bo He, and Jiang Can; 5 qians of Xi Xin; 1 liang of Qian Niu. Grind into a fine powder, taking 3 qian each time. Boil one cup of water, then add the powdered medicine, stir well, and take urgently after meals along with the dregs while hot.[50p]

    　　羌活附子汤 【东垣】 　治冬月大寒犯脑，令人脑齿连痛，名曰脑风。为害甚速，非此莫救。　　麻黄去节　黑附子炮，各三分　羌活　苍朮各五分　黄芪一分　防风　甘草　升麻　白僵蚕炒，去丝　黄蘗　白芷各三分　佛耳草有寒嗽者用之，如无不用　　右水煎服。

    Qianghuo Fuzitang (Qianghuo and Aconite Decoction) 【Dongyuan】
    Treats severe cold in winter, affecting the brain, causing pain in the head and teeth, referred to as "brain wind." This condition can be very harmful and requires this remedy.

    • Ephedra (dried, without sections), Aconite (processed), each 3 grams
    • Qianghuo (Notopterygium), Cangzhu (Atractylodes), each 5 grams
    • Huangqi (Astragalus) 1 gram
    • Fangfeng (Siler), Gancao (Licorice), Shengma (Cimicifuga), Baijiangcan (fried, silk removed), Huanglian (Coptis), Baizhi (Angelica), each 3 grams
    • Fouer grass is used if there is a cold cough; if not, do not use.
      Boil with water and take.

    Duhuo San (Duhuo Powder)
    Treats toothache due to wind toxin, or swollen and painful gums.

    • Duhuo (Angelica pubescens), Qianghuo (Notopterygium), Chuanxiong (Ligusticum), Fangfeng (Siler), each 5 grams
    • Jingjie (Schizonepeta), Bohe (Peppermint), Sheng Dihuang (Fresh Rehmannia), Xixin (Asarum).
      Take 9-15 grams each time, boil with water for gargling.

    Mahuang San (Ephedra Powder) 【Dongyuan】
    Treats toothache from cold fire.

    • Ephedra root (without sections), Ash from sheep tibia, Longdancao (Gentiana), cleansed with wine, Sheng Dihuang (Fresh Rehmannia) each 6 grams
    • Qianghuo (Notopterygium) 4.5 grams
    • Fangfeng (Siler), Gaobon (Old root), Shengma (Cimicifuga), Huanglian (Coptis), Caodoukou (Ammomum), each 3 grams, Xixin (Asarum) 1 gram
    • Danggui (Angelica sinensis), Shudi (Rehmannia), each 6 grams.
      Grind into a very fine powder and apply as previously instructed.[51p]

    　　麝香散　治热多寒少，牙露龈肉脱，血出，齿动欲落，大作疼痛，妨食。　　升麻一钱　黄连　草豆蔻各一钱半　熟地黄　麻黄各一分　益智仁二分五厘　麝香少许　羊胫膏灰二钱　人参　生地黄　当归　汉防己酒制，各三分　　右为细末，每用少许擦牙疼处，噙良久，有涎吐去。
    　　立效散 【东垣】 　治牙齿痛不可忍，及头脑项背痛，微恶寒饮，大恶热饮，其脉上中下三部阳虚阴盛，是五脏内盛，六腑阳道微，脉微小，小便滑数。　　防风一钱　炙甘草三分　草龙胆酒洗，四分　升麻七分　细辛二分　　水一盏，煎至五分，去滓，以匙抄在口中，渫痛处，少时立止。如多恶热饮，更加草龙胆一钱；如更恶风作痛，加草豆蔻、黄连各五分，勿加龙胆。随寒热多少，临时加减。[54p]

    Musk Powder: Treats conditions with more heat and less cold; symptoms include gums and teeth becoming loose, bleeding, teeth moving as if they might fall out, intense pain, and difficulty eating. Ingredients: 1.5 qian of Schizonepeta, 1.5 qian of Coptis, 1.5 qian of Amomum, 1 fen of Rehmannia, 1 fen of Ephedra, 2.5 fen of Alpinia, a small amount of musk, and 2 qian of ash from sheep's hoof fat, along with 3 fen each of ginseng, fresh Rehmannia, and Angelica, prepared with Han Fangji wine. Grind into a fine powder and use a small amount to rub on the painful tooth area, holding it for a long time until saliva is produced and expelled.

    Immediate Effect Powder (from Dongyuan): Treats unbearable tooth pain as well as pain in the head, neck, and back. Symptoms include slight aversion to cold drinks and severe aversion to hot drinks; the pulse shows yang deficiency and yin excess in all three regions, indicating internal excess in the five organs and deficiency in the yang pathways of the six fu organs, with a weak and fine pulse, and frequent, slippery urination. Ingredients: 1 qian of Siler, 3 fen of honey-fried Licorice, 4 fen of gentian washed in liquor, 7 fen of Schizonepeta, and 2 fen of Asarum. Boil with 1 cup of water until reduced to 5 fen, strain out dregs, and use a spoon to swish in the mouth over the painful area; relief is immediate. If there is a stronger aversion to hot drinks, add 1 qian of gentian; if pains worsen with wind, add 5 fen each of Amomum and Coptis, but do not add gentian. Adjust the ingredients as necessary based on the amount of heat and cold.[54p]

    Shengma Powder treats upper jaw tooth pain.
    Components: Increased Xi Xin, Huang Bo, Zhi Mu, Fang Ji, Huang Lian, Sheng Ma, Bai Zhi, Man Jing Zi, Niu Bang Zi, and Bo He. Grind these ingredients into a fine powder, mix with peppermint tea to take internally or apply to the gums; decoction is also acceptable.

    Bai Zhi Powder treats lower jaw tooth pain.
    Components: Bai Zhi, Fang Feng, Lian Qiao, calcined Shi Gao, Jing Jie, Chi Shao Yao, and increased Bo He. Grind these into a fine powder, mix with peppermint tea to take internally or apply to the gums; decoction is also acceptable.

    Shengong Pill (from Dong Yuan) treats swollen and painful gums. If Lan Xiang Ye is unavailable, replace it with Huo Xiang. Each of the following: Dang Gui, Mu Xiang (not exposed to fire) 1 qian, Sheng Ma 2 qian, Sheng Di Huang (washed with wine and baked), Sheng Gan Cao 3 qian each, Huang Lian (remove impurities and wash with wine), Su He Sha Ren 5 qian each. Grind these into a fine powder and make pills the size of a mung bean using a dough made from soup and steamed cakes. Take 100 pills each time, or increase to 200, with white soup when taken, and at a distance from meals. It also treats blood dysentery and hemorrhaging, continuous blood discharge, blood that is brown, purple, or black, and blood in the intestines. Take on an empty stomach with rice soup. For pulses that are surging and slow, it also treats numbness and qi rising, obstructed qi, and hallucinations.[55p]

    　　牢牙散 【东垣】 　治牙龈肉绽有根，牙疳肿痛，动摇欲落，牙齿不长，牙黄，口臭。　　升麻　羌活　羊胫骨灰各一两　龙胆草酒洗，一两五钱　　右为细末，以纱罗子罗骨灰作微尘末，和匀，卧时贴在牙龈上。升麻古本作四分，亦一两也。

    Lao Ya San (Loosened Tooth Powder)
    (From Dongyuan)

    It treats swollen and painful gums, loose teeth, teeth that do not grow, yellow teeth, and bad breath.

    Ingredients:

    • Shengma (Radix Cimicifugae)
    • Qianghuo (Notopterygium)
    • Sheep tibia ash, each one liang
    • Longdancao (Gentian) washed in wine, one liang and five qian

    Prepare the above as a fine powder. Use gauze to sieve the bone ash into a fine dust, then mix well and apply to the gums at night.

    Shengma in the ancient text is recorded as four fen, which is equivalent to one liang.

    Hai Shao Dan (Red Pills for Returning Essence)
    Treats toothaches caused by deficiency fire.

    Ingredients:

    • Rou Congrong (Cistanche)
    • Yuan Zhi (Polygala)
    • Fennel
    • Ba Jiao (Morinda)
    • Shan Yao (Dioscorea)
    • Gou Qi (Wolfberry)
    • Shou Di Huang (Rehmannia)
    • Shi Chang Pu (Acorus)
    • Shan Zhu Yu (Cornus)
    • Niu Xi (Achyranthes)
    • Du Zhong (Eucommia) fried
    • Hua Shi (Paper Mulberry)
    • Wu Wei Zi (Schisandra)
    • Bai Fu Ling (Poria) in equal parts

    Grind these ingredients into powder, combine with honey and jujube paste to form pills the size of a phoenix seed. Take 30 to 50 pills each time, with warm wine or saline soup, three times a day.

    Hei Xi Dan (Black Tin Pills)
    Treats severe toothache due to yang deficiency.

    Ingredients:

    • Black lead
    • Sulfur, each two liang.[56p]

    　　右将锡熔化，渐入硫黄，候结成片，倾地上出火毒，研至无声为度。
    　　牢牙散　治牙无力，不能嚼物。
    　　升麻三钱　生地黄　石膏各一钱　白茯苓　元参各五钱　羊胫骨烧灰　梧桐泪各三分　黄连一钱三分　麝香少许，另研　　右为细末，研匀，每用少许，临卧擦牙，复以温水漱去。
    　　透关散　治风冷蛀龋。
    　　蜈蚣头　干蝎梢去毒　草乌尖如麦粒大者　川乌底如钱薄者，各七枚　雄黄麦大，七粒，另研　胡椒七粒　　右为细末，用纸捻子蘸酢，点药少许于火上，炙干，塞两耳间，闭口少时，即效。
    　　刷牙牢牙散　去风冷蛀龋宣露，用之甚效。　　盐少许，研细　槐枝　柳枝各长四寸，四十九枝　皂角不蛀者七茎　　右同入磁瓶内，黄泥固济，糠火烧一夜，候冷取出，研细，用如常法。
    　　白牙散　治牙黄黑色。
    　　石膏　升麻各一钱　白芷七分　麝香少许　羊胫骨灰二钱　　右为细末，先用温水漱口擦之妙。[57p]

    To the right, prepare to melt sulfur, gradually incorporating it until it forms into sheets. Wait for it to produce a toxic fire on the ground, and grind it until it makes no sound.

    Lao Ya San - for treating weak teeth that cannot chew food.

    Use three qian of Sheng Ma, one qian each of Sheng Di Huang, and Shi Gao; five qian each of Bai Fu Ling and Yuan Shen; three fen each of burned sheep tibia ash and Wutong tears; one qian and three fen of Huang Lian; a small amount of musk to be ground separately. The above ingredients should be ground into a fine powder and mixed well. Use a small amount to rub on the teeth before sleeping, and then rinse with warm water.

    Tou Guan San - for treating dental issues caused by cold wind.

    Use seven pieces each of centipede heads, the stingers of dried scorpions (to remove toxins), large as wheat grains of Chuan Wu, and thin as coins of Chuan Wu; seven grains of male yellow (realgar), ground separately; seven grains of pepper. Grind the above into a fine powder, use a paper twist to dip in vinegar, apply a small amount of the medicine on a fire to dry it, plug into both ears, and keep the mouth closed for a while; it works immediately.

    Shua Ya Lao Ya San - for eliminating wind-cold cavities and providing great efficacy.

    Use a little salt, ground finely; forty-nine branches each of four-inch-long locust and willow; seven stems of non-cavity soap pods. Combine these in a ceramic jar, seal with yellow clay, burn in husk fire overnight, wait for it to cool down, then grind finely for regular use.

    Bai Ya San - for treating yellow or black teeth.

    Use one qian each of Shi Gao and Sheng Ma; seven fen of Bai Zhi; a small amount of musk; two qian of sheep tibia ash. Grind the above into a fine powder and use warm water to rinse the mouth and apply it to the teeth effectively.[57p]

    Musk Tooth Powder strengthens teeth and whitens them. The formula includes 1 part musk, 10 grams of rhizoma ligustici chuanxiong, 20 grams of huanglian, 3.5 grams each of sheep bone ash, white cardamom, and grass cardamom, 3 parts of processed rehmannia and 2 parts of both raw and cooked rehmannia, three pieces of myrrh, one gallnut. Grind into a fine powder and use as before.

    Eternal Spring Tooth Powder prevents tooth wind and promotes dark hair. The ingredients are 50 grams each of chuanxiong, sand ginger, fragrant wood, decoction of various herbs, cloves, rhizoma ligustici chuanxiong, gallnut, poria, asarum, blue salt, alum, sweet wood, white tribulus, and sandalwood, as well as 200 grams of gypsum, nine pieces of myrrh, nine pieces of terminalia chebula fruit, 30 grams of copper sulfate, and 5 grams of musk. Grind into a fine powder, mix well, and brush teeth morning and evening, followed by rinsing with warm water and spitting out.

    Agarwood Powder strengthens teeth and nourishes hair. The ingredients are 20 grams each of agarwood, terminalia chebula peel, blue salt, and indigo, 15 grams each of white sandalwood and mother clove, and 50 grams each of processed angelica and fragrant wood. Remove hair from fragrant wood, and use five grams of asarum without seedlings, and one gram each of lotus leaf ash and frankincense ground separately, 50 grams of bitter neem broken into four pieces and stir-fried. Dragon brain and musk are ground separately at five grams each, and 250 grams of acid pomegranate peel. Grind into a fine powder, use five grams each time, brush as usual, and rinse with warm water, twice daily.[58p]

    Zhusha San: A fine powder for cleaning the teeth.
    Ground zhusha, fragrant grass, mint, clove, cyperus, sweet saposhnikovia, white atractylodes, rhizoma cimicifuga, and yellow dan (each one tael), pig's tooth soap pod (two taels), cold water stone (eight taels), plaster (four taels), white sandalwood, and zingiberis (each five qian). Grind into a fine powder and mix well; it’s excellent for cleaning the teeth.

    Miaoying San: Strengthens teeth, disperses wind, and regulates qi, benefiting black hair.
    Ginseng, fine xin (removed seedlings), white poria, and cyperus (fried to remove hair), chuanxiong, white tribulus (fried to remove corners), and cardamom (each five qian), prepared herbal decoction, white atractylodes, calcined plaster, and dragon bone (each six qian), with a little musk ground separately. Grind together into a fine powder; in the morning, rinse with warm water.

    Dihuang Wan: Treats loose teeth.
    White poria, ginseng, and shan zhu rou (each four taels), goji root (three taels), and raw d黄 (five jin, extract juice), white honey (one jin), and a little oil. Grind the first four ingredients into powder, use good wine (one dou) to decoct until three sheng, strain, then add d黄 juice, white honey, and oil to decoct together until it can be rolled into pills, making them the size of small beans. Take twenty pills with warm wine, three times a day, gradually increasing to five doses.[59p]

    　　甘露饮 【《和剂》】 　治丈夫、妇人、小儿胃中客热，牙宣，口气，齿龈肿烂，时出脓血，目睑垂重，常欲合闭，或即饥烦，不欲饮食；及赤目肿痛，不任凉药；口舌生疮，咽喉肿痛，疮疹，已发未发皆可服之。　　枇杷叶刷去毛　干熟地黄　天门冬去心，焙　枳壳去瓤，麸炒　山茵陈去梗　麦门冬去心，焙　石斛去芦　炙甘草　黄芩　生地黄　　右等分为末，每服二钱，水一盏，煎至七分，去滓，温服，食后临卧。小儿一服分两服，量岁数大小加减与之。
    　　五灵膏　治牙齿动摇。
    　　五灵脂五钱　松脂　黄蜡各一两　蟾酥半字　黄丹二钱五分　　右于磁器中，以慢火熬成膏，用白熟绢上摊，候冷，剪作片子，每夜贴于龈上，有津即吐，悞咽不妨。此药临卧时用一次，于恶硬物底一个牙根儿下，里外贴之，亦不甚闷。若是儿牙坚固，自然得力，不恶硬物也。[60p]

    Sweet Dew Drink
    This remedy treats the internal heat in the stomach of men, women, and children, tooth decay, bad breath, swollen gums, pus and blood occasionally oozing out, drooping eyelids, a frequent desire to close the eyes, irritability with a loss of appetite; it also addresses red, swollen, and painful eyes not tolerating cooling medicine, sores in the mouth and on the tongue, swollen and painful throat, and skin rashes; it can be taken whether the rash has appeared or not.
    Ingredients:

    • Loquat leaves, brushed to remove hair
    • Dried, mature Rehmannia root
    • Venere Lustre (Asparagus root), heart removed and roasted
    • Dried bitter orange peel, pulp removed and stir-fried
    • Mountain artemisia (Chenopodium), stems removed
    • Dried Ophiopogon, heart removed and roasted
    • Dendrobium, roots removed
    • Honeyed licorice
    • Scutellaria baicalensis
    • Fresh Rehmannia root

    Grind the ingredients into a fine powder, take two qian (a measure) each time, mix with one bowl of water, boil down to seven-tenths, strain, and take warm after meals and before bed. For children, the dose should be divided into two parts, adjusting according to age.

    Five Spirit Ointment
    This remedy treats loose teeth.
    Ingredients:

    • Five Spirit resin, 5 qian
    • Pine resin, 1 liang
    • Yellow wax, 1 liang
    • Toad secretions, half a character
    • Yellow cinnabar, 2 qian 5 fen

    In a ceramic container, simmer these ingredients over low heat to form a paste. Spread on white silk and let it cool, then cut into pieces. Every night, apply one piece to the gums; if there is saliva, it can be spat out, and swallowing will not be obstructed. This medication is used once at night; place it under a loosened tooth root, applying both inside and out, without causing too much discomfort. If a child's tooth is firm, it will benefit naturally and will not be adverse to hard substances.[60p]

    Tooth Loosening and Pain Formula
    Five Treasures (Wubizi) 50 grams, White Poria (Bai Fuling) 50 grams, Asarum (Xixin) 50 grams, Green Salt 30 grams. Grind the above into a fine powder. Brush your teeth with it morning and evening for significant long-term results.

    Toothpaste for Loose and Painful Teeth
    Ding Powder and Dragon Bone, each 25 grams, Musk (a word), Yellow Wax 50 grams. Grind the above into a fine powder, mix well, melt the yellow wax, combine with the medicine, and let it cool. Take out a heating iron, spread the medicine thinly on paper. Cut it into strips and place them on the affected teeth and gums overnight. Remove the medicine the next morning and repeat nightly. In a fortnight, the swelling and discomfort of the teeth will diminish, new gum tissue will grow, it treats decay, expels wind and evil, and strengthens the teeth, yielding remarkable effects.

    Wubizi Powder
    Treats loose teeth and injuries from external objects that haven't responded to other treatments.
    Sichuan Wubizi, Dry Earth Dragon (Dihua) cleaned of soil, slightly roasted, each 50 grams. Grind the above into a fine powder. First, rub the tooth roots with fresh ginger, then apply the powder. Avoid biting hard objects for five days. If a tooth has just started to loosen, apply heat to the tooth socket and place the medicine on the tooth, holding it firmly as before.[61p]

    Lu Dou Drink

    For treating extreme heat and persistent toothache.

    • Lu dou (Mung Bean) in any amount, boiled in water until soft, add a little salt or honey as desired. Wait until cold, may be thick or thin depending on preference. Can consume several times a day without restriction. This remedy is not bitter or cold, does not harm the spleen, is good for detoxification, alleviates irritability, reduces fever, quenches thirst, and promotes urination; it is an easy and effective remedy. If there is excessive heat with a sweet mouth, avoid rich flavors; lightly boil to half-cooked and drink the clear broth cold, it is especially effective in alleviating irritability and clearing heat.

    齿门

    　　　　单方

    　　雄黄杀齿虫，取为末，和枣肉作丸，塞蛀孔。　 【《本草》，下同】

    　　齿根宣露动摇：以盐水擦之，热汤含漱百遍，不过五日，齿即牢固。

    Yaxuan Formula
    Borneol and gallnut, three fen each; musk, two fen; red wool ash, pearl, borax, calcined chicken inner golden, calcined human middle white, yuanming powder, indigo flower, ox gall, and honey-processed berberine, all one qian; powdered coptis, one qian and five fen; realgar, five fen; deer horn ash, two qian. This medicinal formula is excellent for treating swelling and toxins in the jaw. Grind finely and mix evenly, then blow into the affected area.

    Qingwei Decoction
    For treating the above symptoms.
    Angelica sinensis shoots, yellow lotus fried with wine, fresh root of rhubarb washed in wine, each one qian; siler, two qian; peony root, two qian and five fen; water, one and a half sheng, decoct for consumption.

    Yuchi Powder
    For treating the above symptoms.
    Dried roots of siler, siler, fangfeng, xixin, baizhi, licorice root, angelica, sophora flower, chuanxiong, duhuo, black bean; water, two sheng, ginger, three slices, decoct, and consume far from meals.

    Tooth Gateway

    Single Prescription
    Realgar kills tooth worms; grind to a powder, mix with jujube flesh to form pills, and plug into cavities.
    For tooth pain that doesn’t cease: grind copper sulfate, mix with human milk, and apply to the affected tooth and cavity, three times a day. Pain alleviates, teeth will regrow, and last for a hundred days as usual.
    For loose tooth roots: rub with saline solution, rinse with hot soup a hundred times, and within five days, the teeth will be firm.
    Peppermint and salt powder, rub on teeth to strengthen them effectively.[65p]

    Qing salt enters the kidneys and bones, strengthens the teeth, and is excellent for rinsing and holding in the mouth.

    For all toothaches: Take two taels of green salt and four taels of white salt, boil four taels of Sichuan pepper to extract the juice, mix it with the two salts into a powder, and apply it to the teeth. Rinse your mouth with warm water and spit it out; it's particularly effective for the eyes.

    For swollen, painful teeth (wind hiding beneath and worms below) with pus and blood coming from the roots: Take the decoction of angelica and drink it, while frequently rinsing your mouth.

    For tooth pain caused by wind and decay: Grind two qian of white tribulus into a powder, mix it with a spoonful of salt, decoct in water, and rinse your mouth while it's hot; this can greatly relieve pain and strengthen the teeth.

    For loose teeth with blood: Take one tael of broken bone supplement, finely grind it, stir-fry until it turns black, then use the powder to rinse and wash the roots of the teeth, and spit it out after a while.

    For exposed gums: Mix earthworm feces with water to form a mud, burn it until red, grind it into powder, mix with pig lard from December, and apply it three times daily until completely healed. Another method: Place it in a magnetic bottle with yellow clay to seal it, and heat it in a pond fire overnight, let it cool, take it out and finely grind it, then use it as usual to brush the teeth.

    For tooth pain from wind and cold, or cavities: Decoction of asarum and angelica for rinsing.

    For cavity pain: Decoction of bitter gentian, rinse three sheng daily, and you will recover in five or six days. You can also cauterize the points on your hand.

    • Toothache from cracks: Grind dead crickets to a powder and apply it to stop the pain.

    Gum swelling and pain: Take the roots of red lantern branch, boil into a broth, and use it for rinsing and spitting.

    Wind-heat toothache: Boil two bowls of concentrated soup from locust tree branches, add half a pound of salt, reduce to dryness, fry and grind, and use daily to wipe the teeth, rinsing the eyes with water.

    For teeth (hidden upper, lower bugs) moving: Take half a tael of salt, two pieces of soap pods, burn them until red, grind them, and wipe the teeth every night. Cures after a month.

    For cavities with continuous pain: Use one qian each of realgar and frankincense, a little bit of camphor powder, and make into pills with yellow wax, forming one pill for each hole. Take an iron rod about fifteen inches long, shaped like chopsticks, with a small hook at one end. Heat until red, leaving only the hooked end, taking care not to burn the lips or tongue. First, use a bamboo leaf to pry open the lips, then hook it inside and apply the medicine, allowing it to melt based on sensation of warmth, followed by rinsing with water—this is remarkably effective.

    For exposed gums: Use two liang of (plant) root, boil in a clay pot with licorice water until soft, remove and dry; add ten pieces of chicken tongue herb, five qian of angelica, and one fen of musk. Grind into a fine powder and apply a little to the teeth. It does not harm the throat.

    For tooth pain: Boil concentrated juice from soap pods and saltpeter until dissolved, then drip onto a stone and wait for it to form frost, and use that to rub on the affected area.[72p]

    　　牙齿肿痛：白矾一两，大露蜂房一两，微炙，每用二钱，水煎，含漱去涎。 【《济众方》】
    　　患齿碎坏欲尽者：常以绵裹白矾石含嚼，吐去汁。 【《肘后方》】

    　　病齿非肿非痛，虚不能嚼食：用《局方》嘉禾散姜煎，食后一服；次以地骨皮煎汤漱之；候空心以羊腰子一对，切片，勿令断，以葱丝、椒末、青盐、蒺藜去刺末，固元散二钱拌匀，掺于腰子内，以豆蔻叶或荷叶包裹，煨令熟，食之，服经两日，顿觉快利，饮食如故。
    　　齿(上匿下虫)肿痛：桔梗、薏苡仁等分为末服。[73p]

    Toothache and swelling: One liang of alum, one liang of honeycomb, slightly roasted. Use two qian each time, decoct in water, and gargle to remove saliva.

    For teeth that are broken and decayed: Often wrap alum stone in cotton and chew, spitting out the juice.

    Tooth pain: Chewing on shrinking sand is beneficial.

    Toothache and swelling: One handful of Artemisia annua, decoct in water and gargle.

    For acute carious teeth: Apply powdered yellow alum, blue alum, and musk. One recipe adds white alum.

    For rotten teeth and gum decay, irrespective of age: Use high-quality salty clay, soak in hot soup to extract the juice. Boil and dry in stoneware, scrape off and grind with a little musk.

    For teeth that are neither swollen nor painful but unable to chew food: Use "Ju Fang's" Jiahe powder decocted with ginger, take one dose after a meal; then gargle with a decoction of earth bone skin. Wait until hungry, then take a pair of lamb kidneys, slice without cutting through, and fill with a mixture of chopped scallions, powdered pepper, blue salt, and thistle, combined with two qian of Gu Yuan powder, wrap it in cardamom leaves or lotus leaves, stew until cooked, eat it. After two days of this, one will feel relief, and eating will be as usual.

    For tooth swelling and pain (with hidden lower worms): Take equal parts of Platycodon and Job's tears, ground into powder and consume.[73p]

    Swollen and Painful Gums: Grind the root of platycodon (jie geng) into a powder, mix with jujube paste, form into pills about the size of a soap nut, wrap in cotton and bite down on them, and rinse with ginger-leaf decoction.

    Swollen and Painful Teeth from Wind: Boil ledum with wine and rinse with the hot mixture. Another remedy: Grind three ounces each of ledum and rehmannia, take three qian, boil with one cup of water, strain, and take warm. Repeat at bedtime.

    Toothache from Wind-Heat: One tael of fragrant white peony and half a tael of cinnabar, ground into a powder, mixed with honey into pills the size of a lotus seed, and used frequently to rub the teeth. This method is said to be far superior to other medicines, as practiced by a woman from a village in Haozhou. Alternatively, one can mix white peony and Wuzhuyu in equal parts, steep in water, and rinse the mouth.

    Toothache: Powdered Qingmuxiang with a little musk, apply to the teeth and rinse with salt water.

    Toothache due to Kidney Deficiency: Equal parts of sweet flag and sulfur, ground into a powder, steep in soup to rinse; remarkably effective.

This is called "Sea's One Character Powder."

    For toothache caused by Wind-Worm: Powdered mountain fern placed on paper, rolled into a tube, ignited then extinguished, and the heat used to blow the medicine into the nose, immediately relieving pain.     Toothache from wind and swelling: Grind two inches of galanga and one scorpion, mix into a powder, then use it to gargle with salt water. This is a proven formula.

    Toothache from wind and cold: Grind cardamom into a powder and place a small amount in the nostrils of both sides; also mix it for saliva. Musk may be added.

Another method: use ground pepper and the flesh of the male gourd to make a paste, and apply it to the nostrils. Another method: equal parts of pepper and peppercorns ground into a powder, make wax pills the size of sesames, and insert one pill into the cavity.

    Toothache from wind worms affecting the head: Fry five qian of psoralen and two and a half qian of frankincense into a powder and apply to the teeth, or use as pills to fill the cavity, daily use is effective.[76p]

    • Toothache from wind: Take monkey head grass, add a little salt, and rub it in the palm to stop the pain.
    • Swelling and pain from hidden tooth worms: Burn purple-blue herbs to ash and apply, five times a day.
    • Bad breath from hidden tooth worms: Grind bitter gourd seeds to powder, mix with honey into pill-sized balls (half the size of a jujube), rinse the mouth with one each morning, and apply to the gums; spit out the saliva – remarkably effective.
    • Toothache from wind and worms: Take half a sheng (about 1 liter) of huluberry, boil with five sheng of water until reduced to three sheng, and use as a mouthwash; the stems and leaves can also be utilized, but no more than three times.
    • All toothaches: Equal parts of wood ear mushrooms and catnip, boil together and rinse frequently.
    • Toothache from stomach fire: Hold a mouthful of ice water, dip a paper twist in rhubarb powder, apply it alternately to the left and right sides of the mouth (close to the nose), and the pain will cease immediately.
    • Toothaches from wind and heat accumulation, and all toothaches that cause bad breath, have remarkable effects. Burn rhubarb in a pot until it becomes ash, then powder it; apply this to the teeth morning and night, known as Purple Gold Powder. A certain shop in the capital specializes in this medicine, and the emperors often redeem it with thousands of coins, with their doors resembling a marketplace.
    • Toothache from wind and worms, with gums often bleeding and bad odor: Soak bitter rhubarb and rice water until soft, then slice fresh rehmannia and apply together; leave it on overnight for immediate relief; reapply if not healed. Avoid speaking, as it may invite wind.[79p]

    Toothache: Use Da Ji to bite the painful area, it works well.

    　　刮骨取牙：玉簪花干者一钱，白砒三分，白硇七分，硼砂二分，威灵仙三分，草乌头一分五厘，为末，以少许点疼处，即自落也。【《选奇方》】

    Toothache: Take a handful of sour jujube, wash it clean, and use forty-nine grains of Sichuan pepper after removing the eyes. Pound them together thoroughly, wrap in silk, cut into the size of bean grains, and place one piece into the painful area to relieve it.

    Tooth and worm issues that have persisted for years, from youth to old age: Use sparrow's millet, also known as du ma grass or cow star grass; take thirty clean bitter gourd leaves, cut the grass into two-inch pieces, wrap them in gourd leaves making five packets, each one inch wide and half an inch thick, and marinate in three-year-old vinegar. At noon, heat two packets in the fire until warm, place one in your mouth to press against the outside of the teeth, replacing as it cools. When you take the packet out and open it in water, you will find worms about three inches long; older ones are yellow, younger ones are white, with as many as twenty to thirty, and at least a dozen in smaller amounts. This method is very effective.[83p]

    　　走马牙疳：小儿食肥甘，胃受虚热，口作鼻息，次第齿黑，名曰崩砂；渐至龈烂，名曰溃槽；又或出血，名曰宣露；重则齿落，名曰腐根。用兰香子末、轻粉各一钱，密陀僧酢淬研末五钱，和匀，每以少许敷齿及龈上立效，内服甘露饮。【《幼幼口议》】

    Malady of the Teeth: Infant's consumption of oily and sweet foods leads to excess heat in the stomach. This results in mouth breathing, blackening of the teeth, termed "Crumbled Sand"; followed by gum decay, known as "Dissolved Trenches"; and possibly bleeding, referred to as "Announcing Dew"; in severe cases, tooth loss occurs, termed "Corrupted Roots." Use one qian each of Lianxiangzi powder and Qingfen, and five qian of Mituo Seng vinegar to grind together. Apply a small amount to the teeth and gums for immediate effect; also take Ganguo drink internally.

Grind to a powder, mix with Bai Fuling powder. Use daily for rinsing the mouth or swallow it; it firms teeth and maintains youthful appearance.

    Pain from Wind Insects in Teeth: Scrape resin from pine, dissolve in boiling water; a rinse will stop the pain, as proven by several tests.

    　　还少丹：昔日越王曾遇异人，得此方，极能固齿牙，壮筋骨，生肾水。凡年未及八十者服之，须发返黑，齿落更生；年少服之，至老不衰。得遇此者，宿有仙缘，当珍重之，不可轻泄！用蒲公英一斤，一名耦耨草，又名蒲公罂，生平泽中，三四月甚有之，秋后亦有放花者，连根带叶取一斤，洗净勿令见天日，阴干；入斗子斛盐一两，香附子五钱，二味为细末入蒲公英内淹一宿，分为二十团，用皮纸三四层裹扎定，用六一泥即蚯蚓粪，如法固济，入灶内焙干，乃以武火煅通红为度，冷定，取出去泥，为末，早晚擦牙漱之，吐咽任便，久久方效。【《瑞竹堂方》】[87p]

    • For toothache due to wind, take a handful of pine needles, a portion of salt, and two liters of liquor; decoct and use as a mouthwash.

    • The Dan of Returning Youth: In the past, King Yue encountered a remarkable person and received this formula, which can greatly strengthen teeth, bolster muscles and bones, and generate kidney essence. Those under eighty years of age who take it see their hair return to black and lost teeth regrow; for the young, it ensures no decline in old age. If one encounters this, they must cherish it and not disclose it lightly! Use one pound of dandelion, also known as double-leaved grass or dandelion root, which grows abundantly in wetlands between March and April, and some flowering in autumn. Take one pound with roots and leaves, wash them without exposing them to sunlight, and dry them in the shade; then mix with an ounce of salt and five qian of cyperus for fine powder, soak these two ingredients in the dandelion overnight, and divide into twenty portions, wrapping each in three or four layers of paper, securing them with six-one clay (earthworm excrement). Following the proper method, dry them in the oven; then, using strong fire, calcine until red hot, cool, take out the clay, and grind it into powder. Use this to brush and rinse the teeth morning and night, swallowing as comfortable, for gradual effects.[87p]

    　　风虫牙痛：橡斗五个入盐在内，皂荚一条入盐在内，同煅过研末，日擦三五次，荆芥汤漱之良。【《经验良方》】

    Toothaches (upper hidden, lower worm): Mash nightshade root and apply its juice frequently. Another method: Burn the wood of an old nightshade tree, apply the ash, and first rinse with a decoction of bee nests.

    For tooth extraction: Soak nightshade in horse urine for three days, dry and fry it, then powder it. Applying it to the tooth causes it to fall out, which is truly remarkable.

    For wind and worm toothaches: Burn a peach twig to extract its juice, then apply a small amount into the hole and secure it with wax.

    For damaged teeth from eating pomegranates: Roast the black skin of pomegranates until yellowed, grind into powder, mix with jujube flesh to form pills the size of tulip tree seeds, and take three on an empty stomach daily, swallowed with warm water, twice a day.

    For wind and worm toothaches: Use a thick piece of myrica root, bake one tael (about 37.5 grams), five qian (approximately 15 grams) of Sichuan lovage, with a small amount of musk, grind into powder, and use five fen (approximately 1.5 grams) to sniff. Hold water in the mouth to produce saliva, which stops the pain. Another method: Combine myrica root, chives, and some kitchen oil clay in equal parts, mash well, and apply to both sides of the jaw for half an hour; the worm will emerge from the corner of the eye, effective when used repeatedly.

    For wind tooth pain: Place five acorns with salt inside, add one soap pod with salt inside, calcine and grind into powder, and apply three to five times a day, rinsing with a decoction of schizonepeta.

    For pain from wind tooth: Use lychee with its shell, burn it to obtain an ash, grind into powder, and rub on the tooth to relieve pain, truly an immortal remedy. Another method: Take one large lychee, remove the flesh and fill the shell with salt, calcine and grind, and rub it on the affected area to stop the pain.[89p]

    For intolerable toothache due to wind and insects: Take a piece of toad venom, soak it in water until soft, add a small amount of musk, and grind them together. Wrap it in cotton the size of millet to bite upon; saliva will flow, leading to recovery. There is also a method using pepper instead of musk.

    Another remedy: Dye silk cotton with toad venom, cut it to an inch long, and place it into the gaps between teeth, avoiding hot substances; it will take effect in half a day. If it's dry, dissolve it in hot broth.

    For cavities: Grind equal parts of herba hirsuta, asarum, angelica dahurica, and dried eggplant, and apply to the painful area. If there are cavities, stuff them with a rice ball mixed with medicinal powder.

    For toothache: Take a rat, skin it, and rub its flesh with realgar for three days until it decomposes completely. Remove the bones, grind into powder, and mix with two grams of toad venom and one gram of camphor. Apply a little to the tooth root; the pain will cease immediately.

    For scraping bones to extract teeth: Take a carp, remove its intestines, place arsenic inside, expose it to the shade until frost appears, scrape it off, collect in a bottle, and use a needle to open the tooth root, then apply a little; coughing will help it fall out. Another method involves placing realgar inside the carp, preparing as before, and waiting for the frost to collect it, using it according to the previous method.

    For toothache: Take a white silkworm (alive), stir-fry it with ginger until it turns reddish-yellow, remove the ginger, grind it into powder, and mix with soap pod water for application; this will stop the pain.[96p]
